 With this one app, you will be able to easily do 17 tasks like booking train tickets, taxi and coolie hiring, booking tour packages, ordering food
 rail mantri suresh prabhu ne guuruuvaar ko railway kaa 2017-18 kaa bijness plan launch kiya, jise mini rail bajet ke taur par dekha ja rahaa he
 During this time, he announced this new app and told that this app will be launched in May this year
 ek pement getwe se hoga sab kaamis project se jude railway ke ek varisht adhikari ne bataaya ki tikat, taxi, i-cataring or anya sevaaon ke liye kai mobile ap uplabdh hai, lekin ab yah nayaa integrated rail ap yatra se judi sabhi jaruraton ko puraa karegaa
 He informed that reservation, general, seasonal and platform tickets will be booked with this app
 iske alaava tikat, vishram kaksh, yatra package book kiya ja sakegaa or kisi restaraan se khaanaa order kiya ja sakegaa
 With this app, you will also be able to find a hotel room
 iske liye kaaman pement getwe system develop kiya gaya he

 dhule loksabhaa seat kaa itihaas
